Se ce non, met sus .ie. table, et le presse ensi com nos avons dit en la gilbositeit, et gise li malaides sus le sain costeit.	And if not, place it on the table and press it as we have said in gilbosexterity, and let the patient lie on the healthy side.
Et quant li dislocations est devant, si covient estendre la jambe malaide hastanment, et selonc ce que j’ai dit; et mette li mires sa paine d’estre sus l’angre malaide, puis presse a l’autre main, et l’estent aval devers lou genoil.	And when the dislocation is forward, it must be stretched out the bad leg hastily, and according to what I have said; and place the mirror on the painful side, then press with the other hand, and stretch downwards towards the knee.
Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les II hainches; et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table; et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz; adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve; et se repose III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus; et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse III jors; puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.	And if the dislocation is to the side, it must not be stretched downwards or lifted from the ground, but should be positioned as if the hip were dislocated to the side, as we have said in our description of lying on two hips; and it should be placed under the buttock, with the ligament stretched as we have said before, and one hand should press at the joint on the table. It will be done when the patient stretches his legs, and they are equal; then adjust the thighs, apply the plaster, and wrap with a bandage so that the hips do not move; and let it rest for three or four days, then remove the bandage and apply the plaster again; and if you see that they are equal, continue to wrap as before for three days; then remove the bandage, and allow the limb to heal properly until the member is strengthened.
de la dislocation dou genoil	of the dislocation of the knee
Li genous est desaluez selonc III manieres: c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier; et ne desalue point devant.	The knee is dislocated in three ways: namely, internally and externally, and behind; and it does not dislocate in front.
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez; et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez; puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les II costez dou genoil forment; et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement; et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie; et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	And the sign is that you command the patient to bend his leg at the thigh, and if it does not fit against the thigh, know that it is dislocated; and for the restoration of all, you make the patient sit upright, extend his leg if he can, and place your back against his thigh, placing his foot on yours; then take his knee with your palms, pull gently between your hands, and form the two sides of the knee firmly. And have other ministers extend his foot until the knee returns to its place, and the sign is that the leg fits easily against the thigh. Then apply the plaster, and warm the leg at the thigh, binding them tightly for three or four days, then release. The patient must not move much until the limb is strengthened.
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez	And if the limb is not in place, administer strong stretching, as we have said in the treatment of the hip, until it is healed.
de la dislocation dou talon	of the dislocation of the heel
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	The heel is dislocated once, and thoroughly reduced both inside and outside.
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee: li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	And the signs are that the ankle is swollen, and shifts forward to the part where it was dislocated: the movement is slight, and one should gently stretch it with their hands when it is only reduced.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville; puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut; et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet; s’elle revient, c’est bien; se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient; et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide; puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet; puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent; puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	And when it is thoroughly reduced, you must seat the patient upright, and have the attendants hold them by the leg above the ankle; then pull the foot toward yourself with your right hand, and twice with your left. Stretch it upward and beautifully place the foot high. Do this twice, as we said, by pulling and pulling the foot. If it returns, that is well; if not, restart the procedure, for it will return. If it cannot return in this manner, have the patient lie on their back on the ground, and firmly drive a stake into the earth between their thighs, tying it tightly with cloth so as not to bind the patient. Then have the attendants hold the thigh, and others stretch the foot by their hands or at the ankle, securing it above the ankle; then stretch each attendant equally, and the stake should be fixed between the patient's thighs to hold the patient when they are stretched. Place your fingers equally on the dislocation with both hands, and have another attendant hold the healthy leg below, and the dislocation will return quickly.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois; puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain; puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors; et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	And when it is in place, put the plaster and plugs over it, bind up well, and tie the foot to the leg, and guard the nerves that are behind the ankle, that the ties not be too tight; then let it remain for two or three days, and as the ties loosen, so does he remove them; then untie on the third or fourth day, and prevent the patient from going about for four days; and if he goes before this term, it is not safety that he will not dislocate again.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if an abscess comes up, it must be relieved as we have said elsewhere until it is healed.
des dois	of the two
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When both are dislocated, they must be beautifully extended with effort, and this is a light matter.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne; et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie; et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the dislocation is in any notch of the back or foot, you must place the patient on a firm bench or on a ii. table entirely straight, and put his foot on what appears from these joints, then press firmly on his foot until it returns; and when it is equal, and nothing appears, place under the sole of the foot a bench for heads, then hold firmly, and let him rest three days, then release him; and make him rest until he is healed.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	of wound and dislocation together
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert: si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis; et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit; et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne; et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis; et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples; et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	When a wound comes with dislocation, and one sees hope for restoration: do not be presumptuous in the cure, if you are not skilled in the art and have not used it long, and if you are not all pitiful and merciful and late; nor too bold. Use at the beginning of things that pacify hot abscesses, and leave the patient to God, if you see no hope of healing; and when you see hope, now reduce the member to its place, as the hot abscesses lose their life; and when the members are in place, administer things that pacify hot abscesses, and cure the wound as it should be with drying ointments; and if with dislocation there is fracture and small broken bones, remove them, and do what we have said about simple diseases; and keep yourself from entering the way of fear, according to what I have said, for this serves you according to your Creator, and for the knowledge that arms and protects you.
Amen	Amen
